SELECT [e].[Id], [e].[CreditProgram], [e].[Name], [e].[TotalCredits], [t].[Id], [t].[ProfessorId], [t].[StudentId], [t].[SubjectId], [t].[Id0], [t].[Credits], [t].[Name], [t].[Id1], [t].[Name0]
FROM [Estudiantes] AS [e]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [m].[Id], [m].[ProfessorId], [m].[StudentId], [m].[SubjectId], [m0].[Id] AS [Id0], [m0].[Credits], [m0].[Name], [p].[Id] AS [Id1], [p].[Name] AS [Name0]
    FROM [MateriasSeleccionadas] AS [m]
    INNER JOIN [Materias] AS [m0] ON [m].[SubjectId] = [m0].[Id]
    INNER JOIN [Profesores] AS [p] ON [m].[ProfessorId] = [p].[Id]
) AS [t] ON [e].[Id] = [t].[StudentId]
ORDER BY [e].[Id], [t].[Id], [t].[Id0]

LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [m].[Id], [m].[ProfessorId], [m].[StudentId], [m].[SubjectId], [m0].[Id] AS [Id0], [m0].[Credits], [m0].[Name], [p].[Id] AS [Id1], [p].[Name] AS [Name0]

SELECT [e].[Id], [e].[CreditProgram], [e].[Name], [e].[TotalCredits], [t].[Id], [t].[ProfessorId], [t].[StudentId], [t].[SubjectId], [t].[Id0], [t].[Credits], [t].[Name], [t].[Id1], [t].[Name0]
FROM [Estudiantes] AS [e]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [m].[Id], [m].[ProfessorId], [m].[StudentId], [m].[SubjectId], [m0].[Id] AS [Id0], [m0].[Credits], [m0].[Name], [p].[Id] AS [Id1], [p].[Name] AS [Name0]
    FROM [MateriasSeleccionadas] AS [m]
    INNER JOIN [Materias] AS [m0] ON [m].[SubjectId] = [m0].[Id]
    INNER JOIN [Profesores] AS [p] ON [m].[ProfessorId] = [p].[Id]
) AS [t] ON [e].[Id] = [t].[StudentId]
ORDER BY [e].[Id], [t].[Id], [t].[Id0]

LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [m].[Id], [m].[ProfessorId], [m].[StudentId], [m].[SubjectId], [m0].[Id] AS [Id0], [m0].[Credits], [m0].[Name], [p].[Id] AS [Id1], [p].[Name] AS [Name0]
